Tablet</h2></a><div class="row MedicineOverview__item___ZtWik"><div class="col-xs-4"><div class="DrugUses__container___2OIRg" id="uses_0"><div><div class=""></div></div><a href="#uses_0"><h3 class="DrugUses__header___29NE-">Uses of Virol Tablet</h3></a><div class="DrugUses__content___38C-l">Virol 300 mg Tablet is used in the treatment of <a href="/diseases/hiv-infection-284">HIV infection</a>.</div></div></div><div class="col-xs-4 MedicineOverview__border___207Su"><div><div class="DrugSideEffects__container___2s-KK" id="side_effects_0"><div><div class=""></div></div><a href="#side_effects_0"><h3 class="DrugSideEffects__header___3PuSv">Virol Tablet side effects</h3></a><div class="DrugSideEffects__content___1XpV9"><div class="DrugSideEffects__block___2yk_W"><span class="DrugSideEffects__label___31JpJ" style="color:#444444;border-color:#EF4747;background:#FFFFFF">Common</span><p>Side Effects of Virol are Fatigue, Headache, Nausea, Vomiting, Ear infection, Nasal infection, Throat infection, Skin rash, Fever, Chills, Abnormal dreams, Dizziness.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="col-xs-4"><div class="DrugConsumption__container___2xDRn" id="how_to_use_0"><div><div class=""></div></div><a href="#how_to_use_0"><h3 class="DrugConsumption__header___1Sqnj">How to use Virol Tablet</h3></a><div class="DrugConsumption__content___3mfDy">Take this medicine in the dose and duration as advised by your doctor. Swallow it as a whole. Do not chew, crush or break it. Virol 300 mg Tablet may be taken with or without food, but it is better to take it at a fixed time.</div></div></div><div class="col-xs-12"><div class="DrugProcess__container___1q7qi" id="how_it_works_0"><a href="#how_it_works_0"><h3 class="DrugProcess__header___2KJQt">How Virol Tablet works</h3></a><div class="DrugProcess__content___232QU">Virol 300 mg Tablet is an antiviral medication. It prevents the multiplication of virus in human cells. This stops the virus from producing new viruses and clears up your infection.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="detailed_information"><div class="InDepthInformation__container___2LPpB" id="detailed_information"><a href="#detailed_information"><h2 class="InDepthInformation__title___rHE_G">In Depth Information on Virol Tablet</h2></a><div><div class="row InDepthInformation__item___3LHOT"><div class="col-xs-6"><div class="expert-advice " id="expert_advice_0"><a href="#expert_advice_0"><h3 class="ExpertAdviceItem__header___3GJKM">Expert advice for Virol Tablet</h3></a><div class="ExpertAdviceItem__content___1Djk2"><ul><li>Abacavir may cause serious or life-threatening allergic reaction. Stop taking abacavir immediately, if you develop such reaction.</li><li>Tell your doctor if you have or had kidney/ liver disease (including hepatitis), if you smoke/drink large amounts of alcohol, have high blood pressure or diabetes, as abacavir may increase your risk of having a heart attack.</li><li>You should not take abacavir tablets with other products containing abacavir.</li><li>Do not stop taking abacavir even for a short period of time; doing so may worsen your condition. </li><li>Do not drive or operate machinery while using abacavir unless you are feeling well. </li><li>Abacavir does not prevent the spread of HIV virus to others through blood or sexual contact. Take the required precautions to prevent transmission.</li><li>Tell your doctor if you are or planning to become pregnant or are breastfeeding.</li></ul></div></div></div><div class="col-xs-6"><div class="styles__video-img___1rCzR"><img alt="video img" class="styles__videobg-img___rgPNi" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/du8msdgbj/image/upload/c_fit,a_ignore,q_60,fl_lossy,f_auto/v1501049248/marketing/og1rzrrcdwcki90sl3su.png"/><img alt="play img" class="styles__play-img___3IrhX" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/du8msdgbj/image/upload/c_fit,a_ignore,q_60,fl_lossy,f_auto/v1501049227/marketing/rvcznkwbne3uejtteclw.png"/></div></div></div></div><div class="DrugWarnings__container___2zc8z" id="precautions"><a href="#precautions"><div class="DrugWarnings__title___3QpKK">Virol Tablet related warnings</div></a><a href="#special_precautions"><div class="DrugWarnings__long-header___1AE5Y" id="special_precautions">Special precautions for Virol Tablet</div></a><div class="row DrugWarnings__content-row___fXi8B"><div class="col-md-3"><div class="WarningItem__container___3kiZS"><div class=""></div><div class="WarningItem__title___2HTPF">Alcohol</div><div class="WarningItem__tag___kgVhs" style="background-color:#FACFD0;color:#B05555">CAUTION</div><div class="WarningItem__description___1Wnw9">Taking Abacavir with alcohol may cause minor drug interactions which may not be clinically relevant in all patients.</div></div></div><div class="col-md-3"><div class="WarningItem__container___3kiZS"><div class=""></div><div class="WarningItem__title___2HTPF">Pregnancy</div><div class="WarningItem__tag___kgVhs" style="background-color:#FEF3D7;color:#997B3D">WEIGH RISKS VS BENEFITS</div><div class="WarningItem__description___1Wnw9">Virol 300 mg Tablet may be unsafe to use during pregnancy.<br/>Animal studies have shown adverse effects on the foetus, however, there are limited human studies. The benefits from use in pregnant women may be acceptable despite the risk. Please consult your doctor.</div></div></div><div class="col-md-3"><div class="WarningItem__container___3kiZS"><div class=""></div><div class="WarningItem__title___2HTPF">Lactation</div><div class="WarningItem__empty-tag___3ZPmU"></div><div class="WarningItem__description___1Wnw9">Virol 300 mg Tablet is probably safe to use during lactation. 
Limited human data suggests that the drug does not represent a significant risk to the baby.</div></div></div><div class="col-md-3"><div class="WarningItem__container___3kiZS"><div class=""></div><div class="WarningItem__title___2HTPF">Driving</div><div class="WarningItem__tag___kgVhs" style="background-color:#F0F8DC;color:#A1AB3F">SAFE</div><div class="WarningItem__description___1Wnw9">Virol 300 mg Tablet does not usually affect your ability to drive.</div></div></div></div><div class="row DrugWarnings__content-row___fXi8B"><div class="col-md-3"><div class="WarningItem__container___3kiZS"><div class=""></div><div class="WarningItem__title___2HTPF">Kidney</div><div class="WarningItem__tag___kgVhs" style="background-color:#F0F8DC;color:#A1AB3F">SAFE</div><div class="WarningItem__description___1Wnw9">Virol 300 mg Tablet is safe to use in patients with kidney disease. No dose adjustment of Virol 300 mg Tablet is recommended.<br/>Talk to your doctor in case you have serious kidney disease.</div></div></div><div class="col-md-3"><div class="WarningItem__container___3kiZS"><div class=""></div><div class="WarningItem__title___2HTPF">Liver</div><div class="WarningItem__tag___kgVhs" style="background-color:#FACFD0;color:#B05555">CAUTION</div><div class="WarningItem__description___1Wnw9">Virol 300 mg Tablet should be used with caution in patients with liver disease. Dose adjustment of Virol 300 mg Tablet may be needed. Please consult your doctor.<br/>Use of Virol 300 mg Tablet is not recommended in patients with moderate and severe liver disease.</div></div></div></div></div><div><div class="MissedDose__container___1FyFR" id="missed_dose"><a href="#missed_dose"><p class="MissedDose__header___1abDd">What if you miss a dose of Virol Tablet?<span class="MissedDose__image-box___1sT-e"><img alt="uses" class="MissedDose__image___1F-qD" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/wpimages/image/fetch/w_20,h_20/q_auto,f_auto/https://1mgstaticfiles.s3.amazonaws.com/skuicons/dosage_icon.png"/></span></p></a><div class="MissedDose__content___29K9-">If you miss a dose of Virol 300 mg Tablet, take it as soon as possible. However, if it is almost time for your next dose, skip the missed dose and go back to your regular schedule. Do not double the dose.</div></div></div><div class="Articles__articles-wrapper___1Nwid"><div class="Articles__container___1u4eh"><a href="#related_articles"><div class="Articles__title___14IxM" id="related_articles">Related Articles</div></a><div class=""></div></div></div></div></div><div id="patient_concern"><div class="PatientConcern__patient-concern___1X3e9" id="patient_concern"><a href="#patient_concern"><p class="PatientConcern__ugc-title___3SMt9">Patient Concerns</p></a><a href="#undefined"><h2 class="PatientConcern__title___1NQA_"></h2></a><div><div></div></div><a href="#frequently_asked_questions"><h2 class="PatientConcern__title___1NQA_" id="frequently_asked_questions">Frequently asked questions about Virol Tablet</h2></a><div class="PatientConcern__faq-card___2Cidi"><div class="FaqCard__container___2UVGr" id="faqs_0"><a href="#faqs_0"><h3 class="FaqCard__header___1TAUu">Frequently asked questions about Abacavir</h3></a><div class="FaqCard__faq-box___10oJG"><div class="FaqCard__question___15-Cb"><div>Q. How does Virol work/ how does Virol interfere with reverse transcriptase?</div></div><div class="FaqCard__answer___ohtlU">Virol works by blocking the function of reverse transcriptase, which inhibits replication of HIV thereby decreasing its level in the blood</div></div><div class="FaqCard__faq-box___10oJG"><div class="FaqCard__question___15-Cb"><div>Q. Is abacavir a protease inhibitor?</div></div><div class="FaqCard__answer___ohtlU">Abacavir is not a protease inhibitor. It inhibits the activity of reverse transcriptase</div></div><div class="FaqCard__faq-box___10oJG"><div class="FaqCard__question___15-Cb"><div>Q. What is Virol/ what is Virol used for/ what is Virol sulfate/ what is Virol-lamivudine/ what does Virol treat?</div></div><div class="FaqCard__answer___ohtlU">Virol or Virol sulfate is used to treat HIV infection along with other medications. Virol-lamivudine is a combination drug used to treat HIV infection</div></div><div class="FaqCard__faq-box___10oJG"><div class="FaqCard__question___15-Cb"><div>Q. What is Virol hypersensitivity reaction/ what is Virol hypersensitivity?</div></div><div class="FaqCard__answer___ohtlU">Virol may cause a serious or life-threatening allergic or hypersensitivity reaction. Hypersensitivity reaction symptoms usually includes fever and skin rash, nausea, vomit, diarrhea, abdominal pain, loss of appetite, severe tiredness, headache, joint or muscle pain, swelling of the neck, shortness of breath, sore throat, cough and occasionally inflammation of the eye (conjunctivitis), mouth ulcers, low blood pressure, tingling or numbness of the hands or feet. Consult your doctor immediately if you experience one or more such symptoms and stop taking Virol immediately</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="DrugInteraction__container___3ydsl"><div function loadScript(src, cb) {
  var elem = document.createElement("script");
  elem.src = src;
  document.body.appendChild(elem);
  elem.onload = cb;
}
function downloadJSAtOnload(cb) {
  var fabricURL = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/fabric.js/1.7.11/fabric.min.js';
  var canvasSequenceURL = '/js/canvas-sequence.min.ce2277390454f0ed7e53be48cac9b3e2.js';
  
  loadScript(fabricURL, function () {
    loadScript(canvasSequenceURL, cb);
  })
}

function onVideoClick(cb) {
  if(typeof canvasSequence === 'undefined') {
    downloadJSAtOnload(function () {
      window.canvasSequence = loadCanvasSequence();
      cb();
    });
  } else {
    cb();
  }
}

while (rangeStart <= 1900) {
  if (productValue >= rangeStart && productValue < (rangeStart + 100)) {
    rangeString = rangeStart.toString() + '-' + (rangeStart + 100).toString();
    break;
  }
  if (rangeStart >= 1900) {
    rangeString = '2000 above';
    break;
  } else {
    rangeStart = rangeStart + 100;
  }
}
